focus_tree = {
	id = brazil_focus
	
	country = {
		factor = 0
		
		modifier = {
			add = 15
			tag = BRA
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = bra_dlc_tree_loaded
			}
		}
	}
	
	initial_show_position = {
		x = 0
	}

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 100 y = 2050 }
	
	default = no

	####### MONARCHIST PATH ########
	## Empower the Patrianovistas ##
	focus = {
		id = BRA_empower_the_patrianovistas
		icon = GFX_BRA_empower_patrianovistas
		x = 85
		y = 0

		cost = 2

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 52
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}

		offset = {
			x = -58
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
					option = HIDE
				}
				has_completed_focus = BRA_empower_the_patrianovistas
			}
		}

		allow_branch = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
						option = HIDE
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {	
						has_completed_focus = BRA_reject_the_estado_navo
						has_completed_focus = BRA_the_path_to_estado_novo
						has_completed_focus = BRA_manipulate_behind_the_scenes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			date < 1936.8.1
		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BRA_reject_the_estado_navo
			focus = BRA_the_path_to_estado_novo
			focus = BRA_manipulate_behind_the_scenes
		}

		select_effect = {
			set_country_flag = { ## that way everything goes according to plan in the event the player doesnt rush for some reason
				flag = BRA_buffer_flag 
				days = 55
				value = 1
			}
		}

		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_MONARCHISM
		}

		completion_reward = {
			unlock_decision_category_tooltip = BRA_patrianovism_on_the_rise
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = "Ação Imperial Patrianovista Brasileira"
				name = "Pátria-Nova"
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_arlindo_veiga_returns_to_rule_patrianovistas_tt
			BRA_add_2_monarchist_support = yes
			add_political_power = 50
			## later on Vargas will establish the Anti-Monarchist Coalition, removing the BoP and political crisis ##
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_vargas_will_form_anti_monarchist_coalition_to_hunt_us_down_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				promote_character = EUYL_BRA_arlindo_veiga_dos_santos
				set_variable = {
					BRA_playing_as_vargas = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					BRA_patrianovista_help = 20
				}
				BRA_clear_vargas_opinion = yes 
				set_country_flag = BRA_hostile_vargas
				set_country_flag = BRA_preparing_monarchist_takeover_flag
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
							option = HIDE
						}
					}
					mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	### Secure the Italian Colonies ###
	focus = {
		id = BRA_secure_the_italian_colonies
		icon = GFX_focus_attack_italy
		x = 2
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = BRA_target_colonial_france
		prerequisite = {
			focus = BRA_target_colonial_france
		}
		cost = 8
		will_lead_to_war_with = ITA

		available = {
			is_neighbor_of = ITA 
		}

		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION
		}

		completion_reward = { ## add claims to the italian colonies and give war goal if not already at war
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT 
							is_claimed_by = ROOT
						}
					}
					OR = {
						state = 661
						state = 448
						state = 449
						state = 662
						state = 450
						state = 663
						state = 451
						state = 273
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ITA = {
						exists = yes 
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = ROOT 
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								capital_scope = {
									controls_or_subject_of = yes 
								}
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = ITA 
					type = annex_everything
				}
			} 
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = BRA_african_buildup
		icon = GFX_focus_generic_africa_production
		x = 0
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = BRA_target_colonial_france
		prerequisite = { focus = BRA_target_colonial_france }

		cost = 10

		available = {
			any_controlled_state = {
				is_on_continent = africa 
			}
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		completion_reward = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes 
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { infrastructure < 5 }
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes 
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes 
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { infrastructure < 5 }
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes 
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_coastal = yes 
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes 
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { infrastructure < 5 }
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes 
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = BRA_establish_brazilian_west_africa
		icon = GFX_BRA_establish_brazilian_west_africa_icon
		x = -1
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = BRA_african_buildup
		prerequisite = {
			focus = BRA_african_buildup
			focus = BRA_build_up_in_liberia
		}

		cost = 10

		available = {
			298 = {
				controls_or_subject_of = yes
			}
		}

		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL
		}

		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					controls_state = 298
				}
				LIB = {
					transfer_state = 298
				}
			}
			LIB = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = BRA_WEST_AFRICA
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
				}
				set_popularities = {
					ROOT = 100
				}
				set_party_name = {
                    ideology = ROOT
                    long_name = BRA_URG_dominion_party_long
                    name = BRA_URG_dominion_party
                }
				hidden_effect = {
					add_manpower = 50000
					add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
					add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					    type = infantry_equipment
					    amount = 1000
					    producer = BRA
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = neutrality
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes 
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Administração Imperial da África Ocidental Brasileira"
							desc = "POLITICS_BRAZILIAN_MILITARY_JUNTA_DESC"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/BRA/BZE_junta.png"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = despotism
							traits = {
								#BRA_disorganized_leadership
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = fascism
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes 
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Administração Imperial da África Ocidental Brasileira"
							desc = "POLITICS_BRAZILIAN_MILITARY_JUNTA_DESC"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/BRA/BZE_junta.png"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = fascism_ideology
							traits = {
								#BRA_disorganized_leadership
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						retire_country_leader = yes 
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Administração Imperial da África Ocidental Brasileira"
							desc = "POLITICS_BRAZILIAN_MILITARY_JUNTA_DESC"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/BRA/BZE_junta.png"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = conservatism
							traits = {
								#BRA_disorganized_leadership
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			unlock_decision_category_tooltip = BRA_the_administration_of_brazilian_west_africa
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							LIB = { is_subject_of = ROOT } 
						}
					}
					puppet = LIB
				}
			}
		}
	}

	### Reintegrate the Cisplatine ### || gains cores and wargoal against uruguay, will also rename states once war concludes
	focus = {
		id = BRA_reintegrate_the_cisplatine
		icon = GFX_ARG_attack_uruguay
		x = 0
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = BRA_invest_in_the_imperial_army
		prerequisite = {
			focus = BRA_invest_in_the_imperial_army
		}
		will_lead_to_war_with = URG

		cost = 7.2

		available = {
			has_army_manpower = {
				size > 119999
			}
		}

		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION
		}

		completion_reward = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = URG 
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					URG = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT 
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = URG 
					transfer_troops = yes 
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_other_country = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 300
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_war_with = ROOT 
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 300
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_war_with = ROOT 
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						create_wargoal = {
							target = PREV
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_argentina_may_intervene_tt
		}
	}

						limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_small_coffee_plantations } }
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_small_coffee_plantations }
					}
					else = {
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_widespread_coffee_plantations } 
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_rebelling_coffee_plantations }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = BRA_rebellious_coffee_plantations_1
					}
					remove_ideas = BRA_rebellious_coffee_plantations_1
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_dependency_on_coffee = 15 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = BRA_dependency_on_coffee
					min = 0
					max = 100
				}
				BRA_update_opinion_variable = yes 
				BRA_set_dependency_on_coffee_idea = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = BRA_civil_war_in_progress
						}
					}
					BRC = {
						unlock_national_focus = BRA_industrialize_fully_our_economy
					}
					BZE = {
						unlock_national_focus = BRA_industrialize_fully_our_economy
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = BRA_rebellious_coffee_plantations_idea
			set_country_flag = BRA_rebelling_plantations
		}
	}
